          <div class=\"col-lg-offset-2\">\n                    <div class=\"wow animated fadeInDown\" data-wow-delay=\"0.2s\" style=\"visibility: hidden; -webkit-animation-name: none; -moz-animation-name: none; animation-name: none;-webkit-animation-delay: 0.2s; -moz-animation-delay: 0.2s; animation-delay: 0.2s;\">\n                        <svg xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\" 85.9c0\"></path>\n                            </g>\n                        </svg>\n                        \n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class=\"row  wow animated fadeInRight\" data-wow-delay=\"0.3s\" style=\"visibility: hidden; -webkit-animation-name: none; -moz-animation-name: none; animation-name: none;-webkit-animation-delay: 0.3s; -moz-animation-delay: 0.3s; animation-delay: 0.3s;\">\n                <div class=\"col-sm-6 col-sm-push-6\">\n\n                    <img src=\"/FrontlineEducation/media/images/absence_lead_time.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"img-responsive\">\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"col-sm-6 col-sm-pull-6\">\n                  <h2 class=\"haze-heading-2-slab\">Insight:&nbsp;Impact of Lead Time on Absence Fill Rates</h2>\n\n<p>Did you know it’s easier for school districts to find substitutes if teachers give plenty of notice when they’ll be absent? Our data shows that with zero lead time, districts can expect a fill rate of just 58%. Compare that to a fill rate of 90% with three days’ notice, or 97% when notified 10+ days in advance!<br>\n&nbsp;</p>\n\n\n\n\n\n                </div>\n            </div>\n            <div>\n                <div class=\"col-md-offset-2\">\n                  <div class=\"wow animated fadeInDown\" data-wow-delay=\"0.15s\" style=\"visibility: hidden; -webkit-animation-name: none; -moz-animation-name: none; animation-name: none;-webkit-animation-delay: 0.15s; -moz-animation-delay: 0.15s; animation-delay: 0.15s;\">\n                    <svg xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\" width=\"100%\" height=\"123.3\" class=\"hidden-small\">\n                        <g stroke=\"#7e4082\" stroke-width=\"5\" fill=\"none\">\n                            <path class=\"linePath\" d=\"M17.5 10.3s0 13.7 0 25.9c0 9.6.4 11.1 4 15.1 3.6 4.1 .5 3 17 3 116.6 0 431.5 0 615.1 0 12.8 0 11.3.9 15.9 5 4.5 4.1 4 5.3 4 15.1 0 8.7 0 16.9 0 36.9\"></path>\n                        </g>\n                    </svg>\n                    <svg xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\" width=\"100%\" height=\"93.3\" class=\"hidden-lg\">\n                        <g stroke=\"#7e4082\" stroke-width=\"5\" fill=\"none\">\n                            <path class=\"linePath\" d=\"M17.5 10.3s0 13.7 0 85.9c0 \"></path>\n                        </g>\n                    </svg>\n                  </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n            <!-- Insight Section 2 -->\n            <div class=\"col-lg-offset-9\">\n                \n            </div>\n            <div class=\"row wow animated fadeInLeft\" data-wow-delay=\"0.25s\" style=\"visibility: hidden; -webkit-animation-name: none; -moz-animation-name: none; animation-name: none;-webkit-animation-delay: 0.25s; -moz-animation-delay: 0.25s; animation-delay: 0.25s;\">\n                <div class=\"col-sm-6\">\n                    <img src=\"/FrontlineEducation/media/images/screening_tools_hiring_confidence.png\" class=\"img-responsive\">\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"col-sm-6\">\n                  <h2 class=\"haze-heading-2-slab\">Insight:&nbsp;Screening Tools and Confidence in Hiring</h2>\n\n<p>Hiring is a time-consuming and expensive process, so getting it right is important. What does our data tell us about districts’ confidence in their new hires? Only 48% of districts who didn’t use a screening tool said they were confident in their hiring decisions. Compare that to 64% of districts who <em>did </em>use a screening tool.</p>\n\n\n\n\n\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class=\"col-md-offset-2\">\n              <div class=\"wow animated fadeInDown\" data-wow-delay=\"0.15s\" style=\"visibility: hidden; -webkit-animation-name: none; -moz-animation-name: none; animation-name: none;-webkit-animation-delay: 0.15s; -moz-animation-delay: 0.15s; animation-delay: 0.15s;\">\n                <svg xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\" width=\"100%\" height=\"123.3\" class=\"hidden-small\">\n                    <g stroke=\"#7e4082\" stroke-width=\"5\" fill=\"none\">\n                        <path class=\"linePath\" d=\"M674.5 10.3s0 25.2 0 22.9c0 9.7.5 11-4 15.1s-3 5-85.9 5c-113.6 0-428.5 0-545.1 0-13.5 0-13.4-1.1-17 3-3.6 4.1-4 5.6-4 15.1 0 22.1 0 35.9 0 52.9\"></path>\n                    </g>\n                </svg>\n                <svg xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\" width=\"100%\" height=\"93.3\" class=\"hidden-lg\">\n                    <g stroke=\"#7e4082\" stroke-width=\"5\" fill=\"none\">\n                        <path class=\"linePath\" d=\"M17.5 10.3s0 13.7 0 85.9c0 \"></path>\n                    </g>\n                </svg>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <!-- Insight Section 3 -->\n            <div class=\"row  wow animated fadeInRight\" data-wow-delay=\"0.25s\" style=\"visibility: hidden; -webkit-animation-name: none; -moz-animation-name: none; animation-name: none;-webkit-animation-delay: 0.25s; -moz-animation-delay: 0.25s; animation-delay: 0.25s;\">\n                <div class=\"col-sm-6 col-sm-push-6\">\n\n                    <img src=\"/FrontlineEducation/media/images/peak_times_PL.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"img-responsive\">\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"col-sm-6 col-sm-pull-6\">\n                  <h2 class=\"haze-heading-2-slab\">Insight: Peak Times for Professional Learning</h2>\n\n<p>Teachers need access to learning that addresses their unique goals. Our data shows that professional learning is concentrated toward the middle of the week, with 47% taking place on Tuesdays and Wednesdays. Consider the effect that might that have on teachers choosing between two learning experiences offered at the same time, or on scheduling substitutes when PL happens during the day.</p>\n\n\n\n\n\n                </div>\n            </div>\n            <div class=\"col-lg-offset-2\">\n              <div class=\"wow animated fadeInDown\" data-wow-delay=\"0.2s\" style=\"visibility: hidden; -webkit-animation-name: none; -moz-animation-name: none; animation-name: none;-webkit-animation-delay: 0.2s; -moz-animation-delay: 0.2s; animation-delay: 0.2s;\">\n                <g stroke=\"#7e4082\" stroke-width=\"5\" fill=\"none\">\n                    <svg xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\" width=\"100%\" height=\"93.3\" class=\"st0\"><path class=\"linePath\" d=\"M17.5 10.3s0 13.7 0 85.9c0 \"></path></svg>\n                </g>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    </section>\n    <!-- End Insights -->\n    <!-- Pick your solution\n    <section id=\"solution-finder\" class=\"hidden\">\n\n        <div class=\"row\">\n            <h2 class=\"white-heading-1-slab hidden\"><span class=\"icon-school\"></span></h2>\n          \n\n\n\n\n        </div>\n\n    </section>\n    <!-- End Solution Finder -->\n    <!-- Product Overviews -->\n    <section id=\"product-overviews\">\n\n        <div class=\"row\">\n            <div>\n                <h1 class=\"white-heading-1-slab\">Partnering with Education</h1>\n            </div>\n          <div class=\"col-md-12\">  \n          <svg height=\"100\" width=\"38\">\n                <circle class=\"stdash\" cx=\"20\" cy=\"50\" r=\"14\" stroke-dasharray=\"0.8,10.1\" stroke=\"black\" stroke-width=\"\"></circle>\n            </svg>\n            <svg height=\"80\" width=\"90%\">\n                <g fill=\"none\" stroke=\"black\" stroke-width=\"\">\n                    <path class=\"stdash\" stroke-dasharray=\"0.5,10\" d=\"M5 30 l1015 0\"></path>\n\n                </g>\n            </svg>\n          </div>\n            <div class=\"col-md-7 \">\n                <div class=\"\">\n                  <h2 class=\"white\">On-demand, actionable insights.</h2>\n\n<h3 class=\"white\"><span style=\"color: rgb(255, 255, 255);
